href="/TuttleYouthSoccerClub/posts/1029438427073431?fref=nf">Tuttle Youth Soccer Club (TYSC)</a></div></div><div class="mtm _5pco" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><div id="id_55132054d3a129d04816027" class="text_exposed_root"><p>Frequently asked questions about soccer</p><p> 1. What does it cost to register?<br /> It costs $60 per player with a $5 discount for each additional child in the same famil<span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">y. Make all checks payable to Tuttle Youth Soccer Club or TYSC.</span></p><div class="text_exposed_show"><p> 2. When does the season start?<br /> The fall season starts the second Saturday after Labor Day and the spring season starts at the beginning of March. Each season is 9-10 weeks, with 8 games per team.</p><p> 3. Is my child old enough to play?<br /> Children must turn 4 prior to August 1st for the fall season. Children must turn 4 prior to February 1st for the spring season.</p><p> 4. How many practices per week and where will they be?<br /> Practices are typically once per week with the younger children and twice per week with the older children. Practices locations and times will be held according to the coachâs schedule.</p><p> 5. When and where are the games played?<br /> Games are played at Wild Horse Park in Mustang. The fields are just south of the Mustang Community Center. Games are mostly played on Saturday with some games to be played on Sunday afternoons. All schedules are written and controlled by our partner club, Mustang Youth Soccer Club.</p><p> 6. What equipment do I need?<br /> A ball, shin guards, and plenty of water. Every player must wear shin guards at all practices and games. Ball sizes are: U8 and below use size 3, U9-U12 use size 4, U14 and above use size 5.</p><p> 7. What does the U in U6, U8, U10, etc. mean?<br /> This is the players age, it means that the player is âUnder 6,8, 10â? as of July 31st prior to the season played.</p><p> 8. How many players per team?<br /> U6 play 3v3, U8 play 4v4 U10 play 6v6, U12 play 8v8 and older teams play 11v11.</p><p> 9. Where do we get uniforms?<br /> Uniforms are the responsibility of the team. There are many local shops and online retailers to choose from.</p><p> 10. My question is not on here, how do I find out more information? <br /> You can get more information on our Facebook page; find us by searching Tuttle Youth Soccer Club.<br /> You can also email your questions to TYSCPrez&#064;gmail.com, TYSCVicePrez&#064;gmail.com, TYSCSecretary&#064;gmail.com, TYSCTreasurer&#064;gmail.com, TYSCRegistrar&#064;gmail.com</p></div><span class="text_exposed_hide">
